## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# big-code-camel-feat-001: Implement camel-fix Component for FIX Protocol

## Task

Implement a new `camel-fix` component in Apache Camel that enables routing FIX (Financial Information eXchange) protocol messages through Camel routes. The FIX protocol is the standard electronic messaging protocol for securities trading, used by exchanges, brokers, and asset managers worldwide.

The component must follow Apache Camel's standard component architecture:

1. **FixComponent** (`components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixComponent.java`):
   - Extends `DefaultComponent`
   - Annotated `@Component("fix")`
   - Creates `FixEndpoint` instances via `createEndpoint()`
   - Manages shared FIX engine lifecycle

2. **FixEndpoint** (`components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixEndpoint.java`):
   - Extends `DefaultEndpoint`
   - Annotated `@UriEndpoint(scheme = "fix", syntax = "fix:sessionID", ...)`
   - Creates Consumer and Producer instances
   - URI format: `fix:sessionID?options`

3. **FixConsumer** (`components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixConsumer.java`):
   - Extends `DefaultConsumer`
   - Receives inbound FIX messages and feeds them into Camel routes
   - Lifecycle management: starts/stops FIX acceptor sessions

4. **FixProducer** (`components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixProducer.java`):
   - Extends `DefaultAsyncProducer`
   - Sends outbound FIX messages from Camel exchanges
   - Implements `process(Exchange, AsyncCallback)`

5. **FixConfiguration** (`components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixConfiguration.java`):
   - POJO with `@UriParams` and `@UriParam` annotations
   - Fields: configFile, senderCompID, targetCompID, fixVersion, heartBeatInterval, socketConnectHost, socketConnectPort

6. **FixConstants** (`components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixConstants.java`):
   - Header constants for FIX message type, session ID, sender/target comp IDs

7. **Build and registration**:
   - `components/camel-fix/pom.xml` — Maven POM inheriting from `components` parent
   - `components/pom.xml` — Add `<module>camel-fix</module>` to modules list
   - Component descriptor files for Camel's service loader

Study existing components like `camel-kafka`, `camel-netty`, or `camel-amqp` for the complete pattern.

## Context

- **Repository**: github.com/sg-evals/camel--1006f047 (mirror of apache/camel) (Java, ~2M LOC)
- **Category**: Feature Implementation
- **Difficulty**: hard
- **Subsystem Focus**: components/camel-fix/ (new module), components/pom.xml (registration)

## Requirements

1. Identify all files that need creation or modification
2. Follow existing Camel component patterns (`DefaultComponent`, `DefaultEndpoint`, `@UriEndpoint`)
3. Implement the component with actual code changes
4. Ensure the module integrates correctly with the parent build

## `camel-fix` Component — Implementation Summary

### Files Created

| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| `components/camel-fix/pom.xml` | Maven module descriptor; declares `camel-support`, `quickfixj-core`, `quickfixj-messages-all` dependencies |
| `…/fix/FixConfiguration.java` | `@UriParams` POJO with all configurable fields: `sessionID` (path), `configFile`, `senderCompID`, `targetCompID`, `fixVersion`, `heartBeatInterval`, `socketConnectHost`, `socketConnectPort` |
| `…/fix/FixConstants.java` | Header-name constants with `@Metadata` annotations: `CamelFixMessageType`, `CamelFixSessionID`, `CamelFixSenderCompID`, `CamelFixTargetCompID` |
| `…/fix/FixComponent.java` | `@Component("fix")` extending `DefaultComponent`; `createEndpoint()` builds `FixConfiguration` from the URI remainder and applies URI params via `setProperties()` |
| `…/fix/FixEndpoint.java` | `@UriEndpoint(scheme="fix", syntax="fix:sessionID", …)` extending `DefaultEndpoint`; creates `FixConsumer` / `FixProducer` |
| `…/fix/FixConsumer.java` | Extends `DefaultConsumer`, implements QuickFIX/J `Application`; `doStart()` loads `SessionSettings` (from file or programmatic config) and starts a `SocketAcceptor`; `fromApp()` routes received `quickfix.Message` objects as Camel exchanges with all four header constants populated |
| `…/fix/FixProducer.java` | Extends `DefaultAsyncProducer`; `process(Exchange, AsyncCallback)` extracts a `quickfix.Message` body, resolves the `SessionID` from headers or config, and calls `Session.sendToTarget()` |
| `…/resources/META-INF/services/org/apache/camel/component/fix` | Service-loader descriptor: `class=org.apache.camel.component.fix.FixComponent` |

SocketAcceptor(this, storeFactory, settings, messageFactory);\n        acceptor.start();\n        LOG.info(\"FIX acceptor started\");\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    protected void doStop() throws getEndpoint().getConfiguration();\n\n        if (config.getConfigFile() != null) {\n            try {\n                InputStream is = ResourceHelper.resolveResourceAsInputStream(\n createExchange(false);\n        try {\n            exchange.getIn().setBody(message);\n            exchange.getIn().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_SESSION_ID, sessionId.toString());\n\n            try {\n                String msgType = message.getHeader().getString(MsgType.FIELD);\n                exchange.getIn().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_MESSAGE_TYPE, msgType);\n            } catch (FieldNotFound e) {\n                LOG.debug(\"MsgType field not found in FIX message\");\n            }\n\n            try {\n                String senderCompID = message.getHeader().getString(SenderCompID.FIELD);\n                exchange.getIn().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_SENDER_COMP_ID, senderCompID);\n            } catch (FieldNotFound e) {\n                LOG.debug(\"SenderCompID field not found in FIX message\");\n            }\n\n            try {\n                String targetCompID = message.getHeader().getString(TargetCompID.FIELD);\n                exchange.getIn().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_TARGET_COMP_ID, targetCompID);\n            } catch (FieldNotFound e) {\n                LOG.debug(\"TargetCompID field not found in FIX message\");\n            }\n\n            getProcessor().process(exchange);\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            getExceptionHandler().handleException(\"Error processing FIX message\", exchange, e);\n        } finally {\n            releaseExchange(exchange, false);\n        }\n    }\n}\n",

<module>camel-flatpack</module>\n```\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Implementation Strategy\n\nThe `camel-fix` component is implemented as a clean, self-contained Camel component for the FIX (Financial Information eXchange) protocol, using QuickFIX/J as the underlying FIX engine library (already present in the project as `camel-quickfix` uses it).\n\n**Design Decisions:**\n\n1. **Simpler architecture than camel-quickfix**: Rather than replicating the complex engine-management pattern of `camel-quickfix` (which manages multiple engines, provisional engines, and startup listeners), `camel-fix` uses the simpler `camel-nats`-style pattern: a configuration POJO, a straightforward component factory, and direct lifecycle management in the consumer/producer. This makes the component easier to understand and maintain.\n\n2. **FixComponent extends DefaultComponent**: Follows the standard Camel pattern. The `createEndpoint()` method creates a `FixConfiguration` from the URI's `remaining` part (the sessionID), then creates a `FixEndpoint` and applies URI parameters via `setProperties()`.\n\n3. **FixEndpoint extends DefaultEndpoint**: Annotated with `@UriEndpoint(scheme = \"fix\", syntax = \"fix:sessionID\")` as required. The `headersClass = FixConstants.class` links the endpoint to its header constants for documentation generation.\n\n4. **FixConsumer extends DefaultConsumer + implements Application**: The consumer implements the QuickFIX/J `Application` interface to receive FIX session events. In `doStart()`, it loads session settings (from a config file or programmatically from `FixConfiguration` fields) and starts a `SocketAcceptor`. The `fromApp()` callback routes received FIX messages as Camel exchanges with appropriate headers set from `FixConstants`.\n\n5. **FixProducer extends DefaultAsyncProducer**: Implements `process(Exchange, AsyncCallback)` as required. It extracts the `quickfix.Message` body from the exchange, resolves the target `SessionID` (from headers or configuration), and calls `Session.sendToTarget()`. Returns `true` (synchronous) since FIX message sending is synchronous.\n\n6. **FixConfiguration with @UriParams**: Contains all configurable fields: `sessionID` (URI path), `configFile`, `senderCompID`, `targetCompID`, `fixVersion`, `heartBeatInterval`, `socketConnectHost`, `socketConnectPort`.\n\n7. **FixConstants**: Defines the four header constants as `public static final String` fields with `@Metadata` annotations for documentation: `FIX_MESSAGE_TYPE`, `FIX_SESSION_ID`, `FIX_SENDER_COMP_ID`, `FIX_TARGET_COMP_ID`.\n\n8. **Service loader registration**: The file `META-INF/services/org/apache/camel/component/fix` in `src/main/resources` (not `src/generated/resources`) registers the component with Camel's service loader mechanism, enabling `camelContext.getComponent(\"fix\")` to work.\n\n9. **Module registration**: `<module>camel-fix</module>` added to `components/pom.xml` in alphabetical order between `camel-file-watch` and `camel-flatpack`.\n\n### Integration with Existing Architecture\n\n- The component follows the exact same Maven module structure as all other components (parent POM `components`, `camel-support` dependency, QuickFIX/J dependencies)\n- The `@Component(\"fix\")` annotation enables auto-discovery by Camel's component registry\n- The `@UriEndpoint` annotation enables URI parameter binding and documentation generation by `camel-package-maven-plugin`\n- The `@UriParams`/`@UriParam` annotations on `FixConfiguration` enable automatic property binding via `setProperties(endpoint, parameters)`\n",
